models.py
```python
'''
Defines the data models for the application.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User
class Event(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    date = models.DateTimeField()
    location = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    template = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
class RSVP(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    guest_name = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    response = models.BooleanField(default=False)
class Payment(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    status = models.CharField(max_length=20)
class ImageStorage(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    image_url = models.URLField()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles requests and responses for the application.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect, get_object_or_404
from django.contrib import messages
from django.http import Http404
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
from .forms import EventForm, RSVPForm, PaymentForm, ImageUploadForm
def create_event(request):
    '''
    Handles the creation of a new event.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = EventForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            event = form.save(commit=False)
            event.user = request.user  # Associate the event with the logged-in user
            event.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Event created successfully!')
            return redirect('event_list')
    else:
        form = EventForm()
    return render(request, 'create_event.html', {'form': form})
def event_list(request):
    '''
    Displays a list of all events.
    '''
    events = Event.objects.all()
    return render(request, 'event_list.html', {'events': events})
def rsvp_event(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles RSVP submissions for an event.
    '''
    try:
        event = Event.objects.get(id=event_id)
    except Event.DoesNotExist:
        raise Http404("Event does not exist")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RSVPForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            rsvp = form.save(commit=False)
            rsvp.event = event
            rsvp.save()
            messages.success(request, 'RSVP submitted successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = RSVPForm()
    return render(request, 'rsvp_event.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
def process_payment(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles payment processing for an event.
    '''
    event = get_object_or_404(Event, id=event_id)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = PaymentForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            payment = form.save(commit=False)
            payment.event = event
            payment.status = 'Completed'  # This should be updated based on actual payment processing
            payment.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Payment processed successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = PaymentForm()
    return render(request, 'process_payment.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
def upload_image(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles image uploads for an event.
    '''
    event = get_object_or_404(Event, id=event_id)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = ImageUploadForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            image_storage = form.save(commit=False)
            image_storage.event = event
            image_storage.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Image uploaded successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = ImageUploadForm()
    return render(request, 'upload_image.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines the URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('create_event/', views.create_event, name='create_event'),
    path('event_list/', views.event_list, name='event_list'),  # Added event_list URL
    path('rsvp_event/<int:event_id>/', views.rsvp_event, name='rsvp_event'),
    path('process_payment/<int:event_id>/', views.process_payment, name='process_payment'),
    path('upload_image/<int:event_id>/', views.upload_image, name='upload_image'),
]
```

```python
'''
Contains the admin panel functionalities.

from django.contrib import admin
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
admin.site.register(Event)
admin.site.register(RSVP)
admin.site.register(Payment)
admin.site.register(ImageStorage)
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Contains forms for user input.
'''
from django import forms
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
class EventForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Event
        fields = ['title', 'date', 'location', 'template']
class RSVPForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = RSVP
        fields = ['guest_name', 'response']
class PaymentForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Payment
        fields = ['amount']
class ImageUploadForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = ImageStorage
        fields = ['image_url']
```

event_list.html
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Event List</title>
</head>
<body>
    <h1>Event List</h1>
    <ul>
        {% for event in events %}
            <li>
                <a href="{% url 'event_detail' event.id %}">{{ event.title }}</a> - {{ event.date }} at {{ event.location }}
            </li>
        {% empty %}
            <li>No events available.</li>
        {% endfor %}
    </ul>
    <a href="{% url 'create_event' %}">Create a new event</a>
</body>

'''
Main entry point for the Django application.
'''
import os
import django
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'your_project_name.settings')  # Replace 'your_project_name' with the actual project name
django.setup()

    execute_from_command_line(['manage.py', 'runserver'])

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the data models for the application.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User
class Event(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    date = models.DateTimeField()
    location = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    template = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
class RSVP(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    guest_name = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    response = models.BooleanField(default=False)
class Payment(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    status = models.CharField(max_length=20)
class ImageStorage(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    image_url = models.URLField()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles requests and responses for the application.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect, get_object_or_404
from django.contrib import messages
from django.http import Http404
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
from .forms import EventForm, RSVPForm, PaymentForm, ImageUploadForm
def create_event(request):
    '''
    Handles the creation of a new event.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = EventForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            event = form.save(commit=False)
            event.user = request.user  # Associate the event with the logged-in user
            event.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Event created successfully!')
            return redirect('event_list')
    else:
        form = EventForm()
    return render(request, 'create_event.html', {'form': form})
def event_list(request):
    '''
    Displays a list of all events.
    '''
    events = Event.objects.all()
    return render(request, 'event_list.html', {'events': events})
def rsvp_event(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles RSVP submissions for an event.
    '''
    try:
        event = Event.objects.get(id=event_id)
    except Event.DoesNotExist:
        raise Http404("Event does not exist")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RSVPForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            rsvp = form.save(commit=False)
            rsvp.event = event
            rsvp.save()
            messages.success(request, 'RSVP submitted successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = RSVPForm()
    return render(request, 'rsvp_event.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
def process_payment(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles payment processing for an event.
    '''
    event = get_object_or_404(Event, id=event_id)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = PaymentForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            payment = form.save(commit=False)
            payment.event = event
            payment.status = 'Completed'  # This should be updated based on actual payment processing
            payment.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Payment processed successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = PaymentForm()
    return render(request, 'process_payment.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
def upload_image(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles image uploads for an event.
    '''
    event = get_object_or_404(Event, id=event_id)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = ImageUploadForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            image_storage = form.save(commit=False)
            image_storage.event = event
            image_storage.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Image uploaded successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = ImageUploadForm()
    return render(request, 'upload_image.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines the URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('create_event/', views.create_event, name='create_event'),
    path('event_list/', views.event_list, name='event_list'),  # Added event_list URL
    path('rsvp_event/<int:event_id>/', views.rsvp_event, name='rsvp_event'),
    path('process_payment/<int:event_id>/', views.process_payment, name='process_payment'),
    path('upload_image/<int:event_id>/', views.upload_image, name='upload_image'),
]
```

admin.py
```python
'''
Contains the admin panel functionalities.
'''
from django.contrib import admin
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
admin.site.register(Event)
admin.site.register(RSVP)
admin.site.register(Payment)
admin.site.register(ImageStorage)
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Contains forms for user input.
'''
from django import forms
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
class EventForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Event
        fields = ['title', 'date', 'location', 'template']
class RSVPForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = RSVP
        fields = ['guest_name', 'response']
class PaymentForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Payment
        fields = ['amount']
class ImageUploadForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = ImageStorage
        fields = ['image_url']
```

event_list.html
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Event List</title>
</head>
<body>
    <h1>Event List</h1>
    <ul>
        {% for event in events %}
            <li>
                <a href="{% url 'event_detail' event.id %}">{{ event.title }}</a> - {{ event.date }} at {{ event.location }}
            </li>
        {% empty %}
            <li>No events available.</li>
        {% endfor %}
    </ul>
    <a href="{% url 'create_event' %}">Create a new event</a>
</body>
</html>

The `requirements.txt` file will include Django and any other necessary packages for handling forms, database interactions, and possibly cloud storage if you plan to integrate it later.

Here’s a suitable `requirements.txt` file for your Django project:

```plaintext
Django>=3.2,<4.0
djangorestframework>=3.12.0
Pillow>=8.0.0  # For image handling
psycopg2-binary>=2.9.1  # If using PostgreSQL as the database
# Add any other dependencies you may need, such as payment gateway SDKs
```

### Explanation of the Dependencies:
- **Django**: The main framework for building the web application.
- **djangorestframework**: Useful if you plan to create RESTful APIs in the future.
- **Pillow**: A library for image processing, which is essential for handling image uploads.
- **psycopg2-binary**: This is the PostgreSQL adapter for Python. If you are using a different database (like SQLite or MySQL), you would adjust this accordingly.

Make sure to adjust the versions according to your project's needs and compatibility. If you plan to use a specific payment gateway, you may also need to include its SDK in the requirements.

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the data models for the application.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User
class Event(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    date = models.DateTimeField()
    location = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    template = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
class RSVP(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    guest_name = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    response = models.BooleanField(default=False)
class Payment(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    status = models.CharField(max_length=20)
class ImageStorage(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    image_url = models.URLField()
```
views.py
```python
'''
Handles requests and responses for the application.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect, get_object_or_404
from django.contrib import messages
from django.http import Http404
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
from .forms import EventForm, RSVPForm, PaymentForm, ImageUploadForm
def create_event(request):
    '''
    Handles the creation of a new event.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = EventForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            event = form.save(commit=False)
            event.user = request.user  # Associate the event with the logged-in user
            event.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Event created successfully!')
            return redirect('event_list')
    else:
        form = EventForm()
    return render(request, 'create_event.html', {'form': form})
def event_list(request):
    '''
    Displays a list of all events.
    '''
    events = Event.objects.all()
    return render(request, 'event_list.html', {'events': events})
def rsvp_event(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles RSVP submissions for an event.
    '''
    try:
        event = Event.objects.get(id=event_id)
    except Event.DoesNotExist:
        raise Http404("Event does not exist")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RSVPForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            rsvp = form.save(commit=False)
            rsvp.event = event
            rsvp.save()
            messages.success(request, 'RSVP submitted successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = RSVPForm()
    return render(request, 'rsvp_event.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
def process_payment(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles payment processing for an event.
    '''
    event = get_object_or_404(Event, id=event_id)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = PaymentForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            payment = form.save(commit=False)
            payment.event = event
            payment.status = 'Completed'  # This should be updated based on actual payment processing
            payment.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Payment processed successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = PaymentForm()
    return render(request, 'process_payment.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
def upload_image(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles image uploads for an event.
    '''
    event = get_object_or_404(Event, id=event_id)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = ImageUploadForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            image_storage = form.save(commit=False)
            image_storage.event = event
            image_storage.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Image uploaded successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = ImageUploadForm()
    return render(request, 'upload_image.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
```
urls.py
```python
'''
Defines the URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('create_event/', views.create_event, name='create_event'),
    path('event_list/', views.event_list, name='event_list'),  # Added event_list URL
    path('rsvp_event/<int:event_id>/', views.rsvp_event, name='rsvp_event'),
    path('process_payment/<int:event_id>/', views.process_payment, name='process_payment'),
    path('upload_image/<int:event_id>/', views.upload_image, name='upload_image'),
]
```

admin.site.register(ImageStorage)

forms.py
```python
'''
Contains forms for user input.
'''
from django import forms
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
class EventForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Event
        fields = ['title', 'date', 'location', 'template']
class RSVPForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = RSVP
        fields = ['guest_name', 'response']
class PaymentForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Payment
        fields = ['amount']
class ImageUploadForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = ImageStorage
        fields = ['image_url']
```

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Event List</title>
</head>
<body>
    <h1>Event List</h1>
    <ul>
        {% for event in events %}
            <li>
                <a href="{% url 'event_detail' event.id %}">{{ event.title }}</a> - {{ event.date }} at {{ event.location }}
            </li>
        {% empty %}
            <li>No events available.</li>
        {% endfor %}
    </ul>
    <a href="{% url 'create_event' %}">Create a new event</a>
</body>
</html>

As the Programmer, you should write a requirements.txt file, which is commonly used in Python projects to specify the dependencies or packages required for the project to run properly. It serves as a way to document and manage the project's dependencies in a standardized format. For example:
requirements.txt
```
numpy==1.19.2

```
According to the codes and file format listed above, write a requirements.txt file to specify the dependencies or packages required for the project to run properly.

Programmer: Based on the provided Django application code, the following dependencies are typically required to ensure the project runs properly. The `requirements.txt` file will include Django and any other necessary packages for handling forms, database interactions, and possibly cloud storage if you plan to integrate it later.
Here’s a suitable `requirements.txt` file for your Django project:
```plaintext
Django>=3.2,<4.0
djangorestframework>=3.12.0
Pillow>=8.0.0  # For image handling
psycopg2-binary>=2.9.1  # If using PostgreSQL as the database
# Add any other dependencies you may need, such as payment gateway SDKs
```
### Explanation of the Dependencies:
- **Django**: The main framework for building the web application.
- **djangorestframework**: Useful if you plan to create RESTful APIs in the future.
- **Pillow**: A library for image processing, which is essential for handling image uploads.
- **psycopg2-binary**: This is the PostgreSQL adapter for Python. If you are using a different database (like SQLite or MySQL), you would adjust this accordingly.
Make sure to adjust the versions according to your project's needs and compatibility. If you plan to use a specific payment gateway, you may also need to include its SDK in the requirements. models.py
```python
'''
Defines the data models for the application.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import User
class Event(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    date = models.DateTimeField()
    location = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    template = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
class RSVP(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    guest_name = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    response = models.BooleanField(default=False)
class Payment(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    amount = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    status = models.CharField(max_length=20)
class ImageStorage(models.Model):
    event = models.ForeignKey(Event, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    image_url = models.URLField()
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles requests and responses for the application.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect, get_object_or_404
from django.contrib import messages
from django.http import Http404
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
from .forms import EventForm, RSVPForm, PaymentForm, ImageUploadForm
def create_event(request):
    '''
    Handles the creation of a new event.
    '''
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = EventForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            event = form.save(commit=False)
            event.user = request.user  # Associate the event with the logged-in user
            event.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Event created successfully!')
            return redirect('event_list')
    else:
        form = EventForm()
    return render(request, 'create_event.html', {'form': form})
def event_list(request):
    '''
    Displays a list of all events.
    '''
    events = Event.objects.all()
    return render(request, 'event_list.html', {'events': events})
def rsvp_event(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles RSVP submissions for an event.
    '''
    try:
        event = Event.objects.get(id=event_id)
    except Event.DoesNotExist:
        raise Http404("Event does not exist")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RSVPForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            rsvp = form.save(commit=False)
            rsvp.event = event
            rsvp.save()
            messages.success(request, 'RSVP submitted successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = RSVPForm()
    return render(request, 'rsvp_event.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
def process_payment(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles payment processing for an event.
    '''
    event = get_object_or_404(Event, id=event_id)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = PaymentForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            payment = form.save(commit=False)
            payment.event = event
            payment.status = 'Completed'  # This should be updated based on actual payment processing
            payment.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Payment processed successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = PaymentForm()
    return render(request, 'process_payment.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
def upload_image(request, event_id):
    '''
    Handles image uploads for an event.
    '''
    event = get_object_or_404(Event, id=event_id)
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = ImageUploadForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            image_storage = form.save(commit=False)
            image_storage.event = event
            image_storage.save()
            messages.success(request, 'Image uploaded successfully!')
            return redirect('event_detail', event_id=event.id)
    else:
        form = ImageUploadForm()
    return render(request, 'upload_image.html', {'form': form, 'event': event})
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines the URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('create_event/', views.create_event, name='create_event'),
    path('event_list/', views.event_list, name='event_list'),  # Added event_list URL
    path('rsvp_event/<int:event_id>/', views.rsvp_event, name='rsvp_event'),
    path('process_payment/<int:event_id>/', views.process_payment, name='process_payment'),
    path('upload_image/<int:event_id>/', views.upload_image, name='upload_image'),
]
```

'''
Contains the admin panel functionalities.
'''
from django.contrib import admin
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
admin.site.register(Event)
admin.site.register(RSVP)
admin.site.register(Payment)
admin.site.register(ImageStorage)
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Contains forms for user input.
'''
from django import forms
from .models import Event, RSVP, Payment, ImageStorage
class EventForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Event
        fields = ['title', 'date', 'location', 'template']
class RSVPForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = RSVP
        fields = ['guest_name', 'response']
class PaymentForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Payment
        fields = ['amount']
class ImageUploadForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = ImageStorage
        fields = ['image_url']
```

event_list.html
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Event List</title>
</head>
<body>
    <h1>Event List</h1>
    <ul>
        {% for event in events %}
            <li>
                <a href="{% url 'event_detail' event.id %}">{{ event.title }}</a> - {{ event.date }} at {{ event.location }}
            </li>
        {% empty %}
            <li>No events available.</li>
        {% endfor %}
    </ul>
    <a href="{% url 'create_event' %}">Create a new event</a>
</body>
</html>

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)

```markdown
# Event Website Builder

A Python (Django) based SaaS platform for creating personalized event websites.

## Overview

The Event Website Builder allows users to create and manage personalized event websites. Users can select templates, track guest RSVPs, process payments, and upload images for their events. The platform is designed to be user-friendly and responsive, ensuring a seamless experience across devices.

## Main Functions

- **Create Events**: Users can create new events by providing details such as title, date, location, and template selection.
- **RSVP Tracking**: Guests can RSVP to events, and users can track their responses.
- **Payment Processing**: Users can process payments for their events.
- **Image Storage**: Users can upload images related to their events, which are stored in the cloud.
- **Admin Panel**: A basic admin panel allows for managing events, RSVPs, payments, and images.

## Installation Guide

### Prerequisites

- Python 3.x installed on your machine.
- Django framework.

### Step 1: Clone the Repository

```bash
git clone https://github.com/yourusername/event-website-builder.git
cd event-website-builder
```

### Step 2: Create a Virtual Environment

It is recommended to create a virtual environment to manage dependencies.

```bash
python -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate  # On Windows use `venv\Scripts\activate`
```

### Step 3: Install Dependencies

Install Django and any other required packages using pip.

```bash
pip install django
```

### Step 4: Set Up the Database

Run the following commands to set up the database:

```bash
python manage.py makemigrations
python manage.py migrate
```

### Step 5: Create a Superuser

Create an admin user to access the admin panel.

```bash
python manage.py createsuperuser
```

### Step 6: Run the Development Server

Start the Django development server.

```bash
python manage.py runserver
```

You can now access the application at `http://127.0.0.1:8000/`.

## How to Use the Application

1. **Create an Event**:
   - Navigate to the "Create Event" page.
   - Fill in the event details and submit the form.

2. **View Events**:
   - Go to the "Event List" page to see all created events.

3. **RSVP for an Event**:
   - Click on an event from the list.
   - Fill in the RSVP form to respond to the event.

4. **Process Payments**:
   - Click on the event for which you want to process payments.
   - Fill in the payment form and submit.

5. **Upload Images**:
   - Access the event details page.
   - Use the image upload form to add images related to the event.

6. **Admin Panel**:
   - Access the admin panel at `http://127.0.0.1:8000/admin/`.
   - Log in using the superuser credentials created earlier.
   - Manage events, RSVPs, payments, and images from the admin interface.

## Conclusion

The Event Website Builder is a powerful tool for creating and managing event websites. With its user-friendly interface and robust features, users can easily organize events and engage with their guests. For further assistance, please refer to the documentation or contact support.
```

# Event Website Builder

A Python (Django) based SaaS platform for creating personalized event websites.

## Overview

The Event Website Builder allows users to create and manage personalized event websites. Users can select templates, track guest RSVPs, process payments, and upload images for their events. The platform is designed to be user-friendly and responsive, ensuring a seamless experience across devices.

## Main Functions

- **Create Events**: Users can create new events by providing details such as title, date, location, and template selection.
- **RSVP Tracking**: Guests can RSVP to events, and users can track their responses.
- **Payment Processing**: Users can process payments for their events.
- **Image Storage**: Users can upload images related to their events, which are stored in the cloud.
- **Admin Panel**: A basic admin panel allows for managing events, RSVPs, payments, and images.

## Installation Guide

### Prerequisites

- Python 3.x installed on your machine.
- Django framework.

### Step 1: Clone the Repository

```bash
git clone https://github.com/yourusername/event-website-builder.git
cd event-website-builder
```

### Step 2: Create a Virtual Environment

It is recommended to create a virtual environment to manage dependencies.

```bash
python -m venv venv
source venv/bin/activate  # On Windows use `venv\Scripts\activate`
```

### Step 3: Install Dependencies

Install Django and any other required packages using pip.

```bash
pip install django
```

### Step 4: Set Up the Database

Run the following commands to set up the database:

```bash
python manage.py makemigrations
python manage.py migrate
```

### Step 5: Create a Superuser

Create an admin user to access the admin panel.

```bash
python manage.py createsuperuser
```

### Step 6: Run the Development Server

Start the Django development server.

```bash
python manage.py runserver
```

You can now access the application at `http://127.0.0.1:8000/`.

## How to Use the Application

1. **Create an Event**:
   - Navigate to the "Create Event" page.
   - Fill in the event details and submit the form.

2. **View Events**:
   - Go to the "Event List" page to see all created events.

3. **RSVP for an Event**:
   - Click on an event from the list.
   - Fill in the RSVP form to respond to the event.

4. **Process Payments**:
   - Click on the event for which you want to process payments.
   - Fill in the payment form and submit.

5. **Upload Images**:
   - Access the event details page.
   - Use the image upload form to add images related to the event.

6. **Admin Panel**:
   - Access the admin panel at `http://127.0.0.1:8000/admin/`.
   - Log in using the superuser credentials created earlier.
   - Manage events, RSVPs, payments, and images from the admin interface.

## Conclusion

The Event Website Builder is a powerful tool for creating and managing event websites. With its user-friendly interface and robust features, users can easily organize events and engage with their guests. For further assistance, please refer to the documentation or contact support.
